Is it a Japanese-British Alliance or a Japanese-Russian Compromise? 102

Although Both Have Difficulties, One Must Be Chosen Quickly

Observations from the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun Special Correspondent

The Osaka Mainichi Shimbun of the 18th of this month published a special telegram from its Moscow-based correspondent, Kiyoshi Kawakami, stating that before 1935, Japanese authorities must choose one of two diplomatic strategies: cooperation with Russia or an alliance with Britain. Currently, the authorities are carefully considering this issue. However, the matter of cooperation with Russia was vague and unclear to me (the Japanese reporter) before I entered Russia. Only after coming here and observing did the issue gradually become clear. Originally, after the World War, the so-called new diplomacy of various countries was only a temporary policy. Now, all European countries have turned to restoration diplomacy, that is, the great powers are making great efforts in the areas of alliances and agreements in order to seek equilibrium. Anyone who goes to the capitals of Europe can hear this constantly. In particular, the secret alliance between Germany and Poland, with Russia as its target, has sought Japan's cooperation. At the same time, Russia and France are becoming increasingly close in order to counter the German-Polish alliance. France has also wooed Czechoslovakia, Romania, and Yugoslavia, forming a Balkan faction. Italy, in order to counter Germany, is working to seize control of Austria. They want to drag the Balkans and Bulgaria into their own sphere of influence. The current situation in Europe can be seen. As for whether the friendly relationship between Britain and Japan can be revived, its situation has also been scattered throughout the European newspapers. Looking back to the early 20th century, when the disputes between Japan and Russia were intense, Ito Hirobumi advocated cooperation with Russia in order to ease this tension. However, Japan-Russia cooperation was not liked by Britain. Because Britain wanted to strengthen its position in China and India, Afghanistan, Balochistan and other countries, it was willing to ally with Japan. With British assistance, Japan could also prevent Russia's southward expansion of power and Manchuria, and the Russo-Japanese War occurred. Now, Russia's national fortune is gradually rising. Should Japan resist the eastward expansion of Russian power and cooperate with European countries, or should it make peace with Russia to protect Japan's interests? This is a major issue at present. If Japan chooses the former, then its target should be Germany. However, today's Germany has been abandoned by the whole world. It is not cost-effective to be close to Germany. Moreover, today's Germany is immersed in European political work, while Japan is reluctant to participate in the European disputes. Therefore, the only country that can cooperate with Japan is Britain. Although Britain opposes the revival of the old alliance, it is expected that there will be no opposition to certain agreements with Japan. Moreover, recently British politicians, newspapers, and naval officers have also expressed opinions in favor of understanding with Japan. However, the trade rivalry between Britain and Japan is very fierce, which is very different from 30 years ago. Today, Japanese products are sweeping the world market, and international politics gives priority to economic relations. This kind of rivalry cannot eliminate the obstacles between Britain and Japan. As for the issue of cooperation between Japan and Russia, there are even more obstacles. Russia is widely suspected by the world, and the Middle East Road has not yet been resolved. It is not easy for Tokyo and Moscow to establish mutual trust. If Russia withdraws its armed forces from the Russian-Manchurian border, and at the same time concludes a non-aggression treaty, it may be possible to appease the situation between the two countries. This is an important policy that Japan must urgently decide on in its diplomatic policy today.

Liaoning Four Townships Volunteer Army Active 103

Japanese Puppet Military Police Unable to Cope

Traitors Captured Will Be Severely Punished

Shenyang Communication: Recently, the volunteer army in the four townships of Liaoning Province has been extremely active. A brief account is as follows: (1) In Haicheng County, Liaoning Province, at around 11:00 a.m. on September 16, more than 100 volunteer soldiers, taking advantage of the Japanese army's live ammunition exercise, suddenly broke into the west enclosure gate from outside the east enclosure gate and shot at the sentries, killing many puppet police officers. The Tengao Fort police station in the eighth district initially thought it was a Japanese army firing practice. Only after a closer inspection did they realize that the volunteer army was taking advantage of the opportunity to act. The police station urgently telegraphed for reinforcements from a large number of Japanese puppet troops, but the volunteer army had already gone to the northwest to fight as guerrillas. (2) East of Xiama Tang Village in the eighth district of Benxi, at around 1:00 a.m. on the 15th, about 60 or 70 volunteer soldiers suddenly appeared and captured seven people, including Meng Xianzhang, Meng Xianting, Meng Xianshan, Cheng Huanwen, Cheng Qinglan, Cheng Qingfu, and Li Chunlu's son, Little Fatty, to set an example. (3) About 120 volunteers from the Sancha River, taking advantage of the tall green gauze tents, attacked the Japanese puppet military police stationed near the railway at 4:30 a.m. on the 15th of this month, fought for three hours, killed more than a dozen Japanese puppet military police, and destroyed several sections of the railway before retreating. (4) Seventy or eighty volunteer soldiers were found in the eastern township of Tieling County. They encountered a puppet army patrol team near Xinglongdian, and both sides immediately opened fire. The volunteer army feared that Japanese reinforcements would arrive in large numbers, and they quickly retreated. (5) In Xigou Village, Fengcheng County, eight miles from the city, more than 100 volunteer soldiers suddenly arrived at 6:00 p.m. on the 15th of this month. It was reported that it was Wang Daguniang's gang. It happened that a pro-Japanese person, An Huimin, was organizing a Baojia self-defense group in the village. The group members at the scene were all unarmed. The volunteer army saw an opportunity to take advantage of, surrounded them, and captured more than a dozen important pro-Japanese figures, including An Huimin. By the time the military police in the city found out, they rushed over at night, but the volunteer army had already retreated. (Northeast News Agency)

The county's Anti-Smoking Committee issued instructions to the various district offices and public security bureaus to investigate and force registration, and widely issued notices, stating that the deadline for smoker registration was approaching and would not be extended. The licenses have been issued by the provincial capital. The licenses are divided into two types, A and B. Type A licenses cost six yuan each, and Type B licenses cost six corners each. Those ordinary people who try to evade the regulations and fraudulently claim Type B licenses will not be allowed. Those who are truly poor must obtain proof from the township head. Wang Bangzhen has been assigned to the first district to issue licenses at the appointed time. Before the end of this month, smokers who have not yet registered can go to the district office to apply for a license. The county's opium den licenses, autonomous region No., are divided into Category A, 157 districts, Category B, 238 districts, and Category C, 46 districts. The contractors have been ordered to pay one-quarter of the fee first and submit it with the special application for a decision. The license fees are 2,400 yuan per year for Category A, 1,400 yuan per year for Category B, and 800 yuan per year for Category C. There have been many applications for sales and smoking establishments in various places, but no decision has been made.

Jiashan

The Entire Village of Ganlu Consumed by Fire 107

Ganlu Village in this county is a large village in the northwest countryside. All the residents of the village are surnamed Qiu. A few days ago, a resident of the village named Qiu Baochuan built a new mansion with twelve large rooms. Friends and relatives came to congratulate him, and the house was filled with guests. Baochuan held a banquet to entertain them. Unexpectedly, at midnight, a fire started from accumulated firewood. In an instant, the flames soared. The Tianning Township Fire Brigade set out to put out the fire. The chief of the Public Security Bureau also led a team to rush to the scene to maintain order and direct the firefighting efforts. At that time, the north wind was strong, and the firefighting equipment was ineffective. All the houses in the entire village were reduced to ashes. It is estimated that banknotes worth five hundred yuan and soft pearls, gold ornaments, and miscellaneous items worth more than twenty thousand yuan were burned. The most regrettable thing is that the Qiu family has been scholars for generations and had a rich collection of books, including some Yuan and Ming dynasty editions, which were also destroyed by the fire god. Everyone who heard about it sighed with regret.

Rickshaw Strike Still Unresolved 108

The rickshaw industry association in this county went on strike because the rickshaw companies restored the original rental fees. The strike has lasted for three days, and both sides are taking extreme positions. Yesterday, Hu Weixin, section chief of the Public Security Bureau, together with Wang Wenjin, a member of the county executive committee, convened more than ten rickshaw pullers' representatives in the county party headquarters auditorium, urging them to resume work to avoid significant losses. After repeated mediation, the representatives only agreed to an increase of five cents per rickshaw to the companies. They would only agree to an increase of one cent per rickshaw starting from October 1st, otherwise, to maintain their livelihoods, they would rather sacrifice to the end. At this point, the situation fell back into a stalemate. Today, around eight o'clock, a small number of rickshaw pullers, forced by starvation, voluntarily resumed work, but they were seen by their colleagues, who pulled their empty rickshaws back.

Starving Farmers Begging Door to Door 109

Jiaxing has been hit by a severe drought, with the fifth district being particularly high in elevation and suffering the most from the famine. Farmers have had no harvest and cannot maintain their livelihoods, so they are taking their elderly and young children to various places to beg door to door. In the past few days, in the area around the South Gate, there have been more than two hundred starving farmers, men, women, old, and young, from the fifth district and Tongxiang, Haiyan, and Haining, begging from various shops. Local figures such as Chu Fucheng prepared rice porridge to feed them a meal and took a group photo to help raise relief funds. After eating, the starving farmers went into the city to beg door to door, a very pitiful sight. At night, they slept in the open. On the 24th, even more starving farmers entered the city to beg. The local authorities have not yet been able to provide them with relief.

Robbers Break In, Steal, and Injure People 112

In the Panjiaqiao area on the border of Wuxi and Changzhou, about three miles away from Xueyan Bridge, a resident named Duan Baocheng, who is over fifty years old, has a son named Duan Jinzhi, who is currently teaching at the county junior high school in this county. The family is wealthy and has aroused the envy of robbers. Duan Baocheng also came to the city for business the day before yesterday, leaving only his wife, Duan Yinshi, his daughter, Duan Pinzhen, and a maid at home. Unexpectedly, at around twelve o'clock at night, more than ten robbers suddenly came, each holding guns and weapons, broke down the door, and ransacked the house at will. They also burned Duan Yinshi's hair, causing serious injuries. After half an hour, they fled with their loot. Before leaving, they fired a shot, wounding Duan Yinshi's right foot. After checking, it was found that clothes, jewelry, cash, and other items worth about six hundred yuan were stolen. The Xueyan Bridge Security Regiment has been notified to investigate and recover the stolen goods. Also, in the Hua Da Fang Village in the third district of the county, at around ten o'clock the night before last, several bandit boats sailed in from Daxi Bridge on Taihu Lake, firing shots to show their power, intending to rob. The villagers there rang gongs to alert the others and separately telegraphed the county government on behalf of the Public Security Bureau and the eighth branch of the Public Security Bureau in charge. Security teams, detective teams, patrol car teams, and detectives from the Supervision Office were dispatched to the countryside to arrest the bandits. Seeing that they could not succeed, the bandits hoisted their sails and fled, so the local area did not suffer any losses.

Once the province resolves the issue, they will comply with the regulations and pay the tax. The reasons they gave were roughly that the tax was changed from being handled by the ministry to being handled by the province, and the contractor was the Joint Association of Tobacco and Alcohol Industry Associations of Shanghai, Nanjing, and Suzhou, in the hope of reducing the burden and alleviating business difficulties. Unexpectedly, the situation worsened, and the new tax amount exceeded that of the southern Jiangsu counties. If they could afford it, it would be a matter of provincial tax, and they should勉繳 [Reluctantly Pay]. However, with the bankruptcy of the countryside and the decline of commerce, it is difficult to maintain the original amount, let alone increase it, and the increase is particularly heavy in northern Jiangsu. Such unfairness is too great. In addition to the joint office established by the tobacco and alcohol industry associations of the twenty-seven counties in northern Jiangsu in Huaiyin, Wang Jinting, Liu Dingxin, and others were publicly elected to go to the province to petition. Your association should submit a request to the county and forward it to the Department, ordering them to collect the tax as before to alleviate business difficulties, and requesting the county to assist in the collection of the tax after the provincial government resolves the issue. The county government has instructed the Chamber of Commerce that, as the case concerns provincial taxes, this government cannot forward the request and should be informed accordingly.

Villagers Gather to Eat 118

In the Nianmiao Bridge area of the sixth district, Zhang Xintian, who runs a tea stall, has a small fortune and has accumulated considerable wealth. The cotton stalks were damaged, and the seed pods did not form, resulting in no harvest, making life difficult. At this time of year, when the old harvest is exhausted and the new harvest is not yet ready, many people are in danger of running out of food. On the 23rd, as many as three or four hundred village women led their elderly and young children to Zhang's house to eat. The rice and grain in the barn were all freely cooked and eaten. Because there were so many people, the Zhang family could not do anything. They then persuaded the crowd in a roundabout way and gave each person ten copper coins before they dispersed. The Mid-Autumn Festival Market is Quiet 119

The abolished lunar Mid-Autumn Festival is traditionally a time for settling accounts in the second period of the year for various industries. Here, we follow the usual custom, without exception. All the shops, big and small, are extremely busy settling accounts and making payments, and the market is also relatively lively. However, due to the scarcity of crops in recent years and the economic decline, various sectors are showing signs of depression. As a result, collection and payment are difficult, and all industries are pulling together, accounting for about 30-40% of the total. Even the most successful incense and candle shops and tea and food shops (selling mooncakes) have seen a decline. There are many incense stands that are unsold. Mooncake shops usually close in the afternoon on this day, indicating that their goods have been sold out. This year, however, at eight o'clock in the evening, mooncake boxes were still piled high on the shelves, indicating that the social economy is tight, and the purchasing power is weak, making it difficult to satisfy the elegant interest in enjoying the moon.

Local News

National Congress of the Chinese Red Cross Society Opened Yesterday 127

A Total of 164 Representatives from Various Regions Attended

Personnel from the Ministry of Interior and Other Agencies Were Sent to Participate

The Conference is Scheduled for Four Days, and Meetings Will Continue This Morning

The Chinese Red Cross Society held its first National Congress of Members' Representatives in the Grand Auditorium of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday morning, starting at 9:00 AM. The conference was scheduled for four days. A total of 164 people attended, including Gan Naiguang, representative of the Ministry of Interior and Vice Minister; Yang Hui, representative of the Ministry of Military Affairs; Chen Tai'ao, representative of the Ministry of Navy; Zhao Tiezhang, representative of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs; and Wang Peiyuan, Chairman of the Red Cross Society. During the opening ceremony, representatives from various agencies delivered speeches. The meeting continued intermittently at 2:00 PM, and discussions on proposals began. The details are recorded as follows:

Hall Arrangement: The meeting hall was located in the Grand Auditorium of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce near the Tianhou Palace Bridge. A Party-State flag and a white cloth banner reading "First National Congress of Members' Representatives of the Chinese Red Cross Society" were hung above the main entrance. Inside the hall, a portrait of the late Founding Father Sun Yat-sen was hung in the center of the stage, flanked by Party-State flags. Seats were arranged for representatives from various ministries, standing committee members, news reporters, and recorders. The national flags of various countries were hung in a cross shape in the center. Red Cross white cloth flags were hung all around the hall, creating a simple yet magnificent atmosphere.

Attending Representatives: Yesterday's attending representatives included Wen Lanting, Guan Jiongzhi, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Peiyuan, Lin Kanghou, Shen Lianfang, Wu Xiaolai, Gu Xinyi, Hong Yanbin, Dong Xinqin, Yu Chengmei, Kan Zongji, Li Yingfu, Wang Zhenchuan, Liu Ben Du, Liu Xingwu, Qin Yaojiang, Yao Yuqin, Dong Jingren, Xu Ke, Ji Zhuzhuqing, Zhou Guangjiu, Wang Jin Yuan, Wang Fu Dong, Wu Weinong, Jiang Mao Heng, Zhou Huiwen, Wang Pingru, Huang Liang Kui, and others, totaling 164 people, as well as Gan Naiguang, Vice Minister of the Ministry of Interior, Cao Zhonglin, Section Chief of the Fourth Section of the Civil Affairs Department, Chen Hui, Committee Member of the Military Medical Design and Supervision Committee of the Military Affairs Commission, Zhao Tiezhang, Section Chief of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and Chen Tai'ao, Section Chief of the Ministry of Navy, etc.

Chairman's Report: After the formal salutations, Wen Lanting, the temporary chairman, delivered a report, stating that Mr. Wang Yiting was unable to attend due to illness and had entrusted him to represent him. He expressed gratitude to the representatives for traveling from afar to gather and discuss future plans for the association, and to the military and political authorities for their guidance. He anticipated that this unprecedented event would yield satisfactory results and hoped that all representatives would express their views to improve the association's work.

Internal Admonition: After the chairman's report, Gan Naiguang, Vice Minister of the Ministry of Interior, delivered a speech, stating that the Chinese Red Cross Society was established in the 30th year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty, which is now thirty years ago. In these thirty years, it has convened two national member congresses and one special congress, all held in accordance with the association's charter. On December 6th of the 21st year, the National Government promulgated the "Regulations for the Administration of the Red Cross Society of the Republic of China." On June 3rd of the following year, the Executive Yuan promulgated the "Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Regulations," which stipulated that the Red Cross Society of the Republic of China, as designated by the Ministries of Military Affairs and Navy, should assist the rear service health work of the army, navy, and air force during wartime, and, as designated by the Ministries of Interior and Foreign Affairs, should be responsible for disaster relief, medical treatment, and other rescue matters both domestically and internationally. It also stipulated the establishment of a general headquarters and branch offices. The Ministry of Interior was designated as the competent authority for the general headquarters, which was also subject to the supervision of the Ministries of Foreign Affairs, Military Affairs, and Navy. The branch offices were subordinate to the general headquarters, with the local administrative authorities as the competent authority. The regulations also stipulated that the directors and supervisors of the general headquarters should be appointed by the National Government upon recommendation by the ministries. All the tasks that the Red Cross Society should undertake in peacetime and wartime, the relationship between the general headquarters and the central ministries, the relationship between the general headquarters and the branch offices and local administrative authorities, and the appointment of supervisors and directors were all clearly defined by law. With such heavy responsibilities, the government's expectations are even greater. The Ministry deeply believes that the Red Cross Society is of great importance to the national standing and the welfare of the people. Without thorough reforms, it will be difficult to achieve rapid development. Therefore, the Ministry has sent personnel to Shanghai for inspection and instructed the general headquarters to convene the first National Congress of Members' Representatives on a regular basis in accordance with the law, so as to gather comrades from all over the country, carefully select responsible personnel, and establish permanent plans to promote the cause of the Red Cross Society of the Republic of China. Now that it has been held as scheduled, the Ministry is truly gratified. Here, I would like to list the Ministry's hopes for all of you attending the meeting: The Red Cross Society stands in a detached position and is responsible for providing assistance in times of war or disaster. This is a universally recognized principle. Although the Chinese Red Cross Society has made considerable efforts in the past, it lacks sufficient reserves of relief materials in peacetime and adequate training of relief personnel. In the event of an incident, it is often unable to cope adequately. The Ministry has instructed the general headquarters to draft a detailed plan for establishing hospitals, stockpiling relief materials, and training relief personnel, and to send it to the branch offices in advance for comments. The general headquarters has sorted them out and submitted them to the congress for discussion. I sincerely hope that the representatives will carefully review and agree on detailed measures and instruct the general headquarters to work hard to implement them. This is the first sincere hope that the Ministry has for the congress. The Red Cross Society of the Republic of China needs to have a complete and strict organization to fulfill its mission. The so-called strict organization not only requires the general headquarters and branch offices to be reorganized separately in accordance with the law and to elect responsible personnel, but also requires close contact between the general headquarters and the branch offices. The business and accounting of the branch offices must be subject to the supervision of the general headquarters, and the general headquarters must pay attention to guiding the branch offices at any time. The Ministry has instructed the general headquarters to draft the articles of association of the general headquarters and the branch offices and submit them to the congress for review. These articles of association embody the organizational spirit of the Red Cross Society of the Republic of China, and all members and staff must abide by them without fail. I sincerely hope that the representatives will do their best to deliberate and agree on them properly. This is the second sincere hope that the Ministry has for the congress. The progress of every undertaking must first establish its financial foundation. This is a principle that is not easy to follow. The annual income and expenditure of the Red Cross Society of the Republic of China is no less than one million yuan. Whether the use of this money is proper and whether the income and expenditure are extravagant or wasteful requires a complete budgetary system and accounting organization, as well as an accounting inspection system, to sort it out. This is the key to the success or failure of the association's affairs and cannot be ignored. The accounts of the general headquarters have been inspected by accountants appointed by the Ministry to increase public trust. The Ministry has sent personnel to supervise the general headquarters to draft the accounting regulations of the general headquarters and the branch offices for implementation. However, the general headquarters and the branch offices have many undertakings and limited funds. How can income and expenditure be matched and budgets balanced in the future? These all need to be carefully explored. This is the third sincere hope that the Ministry has for the congress. The Red Cross Society should make every effort to solicit members widely as a fundamental requirement for completing all its plans. The Red Cross Society of the Republic of China currently has only more than 100,000 members, which is too few. It should strive to solicit members in the near future, at least 1 million people. It should also pay attention to soliciting young members, so that young people can understand the spirit of the Red Cross Society, develop their personal health habits, and train to serve the community. On the one hand, it should strive to publicize the cause of the Red Cross Society and health education to gain the trust of the people. All these matters need to be discussed and agreed upon separately in a detailed plan, and the general headquarters should be responsible for implementation. This is the fourth sincere hope that the Ministry has for the congress. All the representatives of the congress have been elected from all over the country and have been planning the development of the association's affairs for a long time. I deeply hope that everyone will do their best, work together in harmony, move forward courageously, promote the cause of social relief, and enhance the spirit of mutual assistance among human beings. This is what I earnestly hope for.

Representative Speech: After Gan's speech, Chen Hui, the representative of the Military Affairs Commission, delivered a speech, stating that the Red Cross Society has been established for more than 30 years and can be said to be the only international charitable organization in China. The work it has served in the past has been based on the spirit of sacrifice and has created great achievements. The Red Cross Society has made outstanding achievements in serving during wartime. Therefore, the Red Cross Society has a very close relationship with the military. Whenever a war occurs, the Red Cross Society always serves in the rear, and the local area benefits greatly. Therefore, all the work of the Red Cross Society is based on a humanitarian standpoint and aims to serve. Its spirit of sacrifice and risk-taking should be admired by us. In the future, if it can cooperate with the government and work together, the association's affairs will have a brighter future. Chen Tai'ao, representative of the Ministry of Navy, delivered a speech, stating that all the representatives are enthusiastic philanthropists. The work of your association has made great contributions to the country and society. I sincerely hope that your colleagues will continue to work hard in this spirit. The humanism and the principle of serving the public proposed by Vice Minister Gan are especially the compass that your association should have. Zhao Tiezhang, representative of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, delivered a speech, stating that the Red Cross Society has a long history, and with a unified organization in the future, its work can increase efficiency a lot. The Red Cross Society has always taken universal love as its mission. In recent years, the international situation has become increasingly urgent. In my opinion, more attention should be paid to the work of ending wars and promoting world peace. After the representatives finished their speeches, they elected Wen Lanting, Guan Jiongzhi, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Peiyuan, Lin Kanghou, Shen Lianfang, and Wang Xiaolai to form the presidium. It was noon, so lunch was served. The meeting continued at 2:00 PM in the afternoon.

Ministry of Finance Plans to Build Salt Warehouses on the Four Shores 128

Approved to be Collected from Salt Tax

The Decision to Cancel the Sail Transport at Twelve Forts Will Be Gradually Implemented

Plans to Open a Sack Factory to Relieve Sailors: According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the Ministry of Finance is preparing to build salt warehouses on the four shores. The cancellation of sail transport at Twelve Forts is being gradually implemented due to the opposition of transport workers. Xin Sheng News Agency reporters learned the following details from the General Inspectorate of Salt Affairs yesterday:

Building Warehouses: The Salt Affairs Administration is determined to cancel the sail transport at Twelve Forts and use steamers to reach the four shores directly. As for the detailed plan for building salt warehouses on the four shores, it has been prepared by Commissioner Miao and is now being prepared for construction. It is decided to build: (1) three warehouses on the Xiang shore: Yuezhou, Changsha, Hengyang; (2) two warehouses on the E shore: Hankou, Xinti; (3) two warehouses on the West shore: Jiujiang, Hukou; (4) two warehouses on the Wan shore: Datong, Wuhu. The construction costs will be collected from the salt tax.

Cancelling Sail Transport: The salt produced in the salt-producing areas of Jiangsu Province, such as Banpu, Chenjiagang, Duigou, Yanweigang, etc., was originally transported by steamer to Twelve Forts, and then transported by sail from Twelve Forts to the four shores. In the first year of the Republic of China, the salt affairs authorities planned to cancel sail transport and use steamers directly, but it was suspended due to the opposition of the sail transport workers. Now the Salt Affairs Administration is determined to cancel it, provide relief to the sail transport workers, and plans to open a sack factory to accommodate the sail transport workers. Because sacks are the most suitable for packing salt, although the sail transport workers insist on opposing it, it has been delayed and has not been implemented yet. The Salt Affairs Administration believes that the sail transport workers' opposition is unreasonable, so it has decided to implement it gradually.

The Salt Affairs Inspectorate Sends Personnel to Bengbu to Thoroughly Investigate the Salt Disturbance 129

And Deal with it Opportunistically to Seek a Solution

Decision to Collect Taxes for the Construction of Salt Warehouses

According to the Dagong News Agency, the salt disturbance in the Bengbu salt area is very intense, and the situation is becoming increasingly serious. The General Inspectorate of Salt Affairs of the Ministry of Finance specially sent commissioners Lu Siden and Jin Xiangsheng to Bengbu yesterday to investigate and find ways to mediate. Dagong News Agency reporters interviewed Secretary Shen of the Inspectorate General Office yesterday, who gave the following details:

The Cause of the Disturbance is Investment Competition: The cause of this salt disturbance in the Bengbu salt area has been rumored, and the reports in various newspapers have many misunderstandings about the truth of the cause. In fact, the most important cause of the disturbance is the loan incident between salt merchants and the banking industry, and the salt affairs agencies are secondary. The amount of salt entering and leaving Bengbu each year is very large. The banking industry is happy to invest in this kind of fixed production business. Initially, only the Bank of China invested, and later the Shanghai Bank, Zhejiang Xingye Bank, Jiangsu Bank, etc. successively invested in the salt area and loaned money to salt merchants, competing with each other. This year, due to the increase in salt production and the decrease in sales, merchants and people in the salt area unanimously demanded that banks invest and reduce loan interest rates. The banks insisted on the original rules, so the dispute brewed and became increasingly profound. The Bengbu Salt Affairs Inspection Office was afraid that both sides would tend to extremes and affect tax revenue, so it tried to mediate, but both sides refused to give in, and the salt merchants misunderstood the official interference, so it caused a serious disturbance. This is the inside story of the cause of the disturbance.

Sending Personnel to Investigate and Deal with it Opportunistically: Since the salt merchants misunderstood and caused the disturbance, the Ministry of Finance believed that the conflict between the investing banks and the merchants and people in the salt area was unresolved for a long time, which indirectly affected the national tax revenue. It instructed the office to conduct mediation, so it specially sent Deputy Inspector General Lu Siden and Jin Xiangsheng, former tax commissioner of Bengbu and current manager of the Yangzhou Inspection Office, to Bengbu yesterday to investigate. The two commissioners are very harmonious with the merchants and people in the Bengbu salt area and are very familiar with the local situation. Although they are tasked with investigating the disturbance, they can find ways to mediate when necessary and will probably be able to solve it soon.

Collecting Taxes for the Construction of Salt Warehouses: Finally, the reporter asked whether the Ministry of Finance planned to borrow 10 million yuan from the banking industry to build salt storage warehouses and develop the salt area. Secretary Shen replied that this news was a rumor and was not true. He had already clarified it. However, the construction of salt warehouses in Bengbu is indeed planned, and the expenses will not be borrowed from the banking industry, but will only be collected from the salt area to be used as construction expenses. The method of collecting taxes still needs to be submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval before it can be implemented. At present, the disturbance has not been resolved, and the salt warehouse plan has been put on hold for the time being, to be carried out after the disturbance subsides.

News from National Exhibitions Around the Country 133

Yangzhou National Exhibition Closes Today

Jiangxi Requests Reduced Transportation Costs and Tax Exemption

Zhenjiang Ends with a Summary of Income and Expenses

The Shanghai Chinese National Products Manufacturers Association, recently because the Yangzhou National Products Exhibition is closing today, has specially initiated the Jiangxi Provincial Capital National Products Exhibition. Since the preparation, participating manufacturers have been very enthusiastic. Also, all income and expenditure accounts of the Zhenjiang National Exhibition have been settled and reported separately. The following are details from a reporter of the Xin Sheng News Agency:

Request for Reduced Transportation Costs and Tax Exemption: The association believes that since the exhibition of national products is mainly for promotion, it should make every effort to seek cost savings for the participating manufacturers of the Jiangxi exhibition. Yesterday, the association specially submitted a request to the Ministry of Communications, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Railways for the issuance of reduced-fare transportation orders and free orders, as well as reduced boat and train fares, to ease the burden on various factories and maximize promotion. The original text is as follows: "Submitting a request for holding the Jiangxi Provincial Capital National Products Exhibition, humbly requesting the granting of reduced-fare (tax-exemption orders) to facilitate the promotion of national products. We believe that promoting national products places primary importance on promotion. National products exhibitions are the most effective way to promote national products. This association, recognizing the importance of promoting national products, has initiated the Jiangxi Provincial Capital National Products Exhibition to provide people in the interior with the opportunity to recognize national products and arouse their interest in using them. We have already sent personnel to Jiangxi to negotiate properly and have repeatedly received letters and telegrams of welcome from various sectors of the Jiangxi provincial party and government, and have designated Nanchang Dacheng Park as the venue. This association has already begun preparations. However, since the exhibition of national products is mainly for promotion, it is different from commercial profiteering. The expenses of participating manufacturers should be reduced as much as possible to lighten their burden and maximize promotion. Now, the distance between Shanghai and Jiangxi Province is far, and the cost of traveling by boat and train is quite high. If the transportation costs for participating manufacturers are the same as those for ordinary stores, the burden will be too heavy. Therefore, we specially submit this document to your ministry, humbly requesting the granting of reduced-fare transportation orders and tax-exemption orders, and requesting that state-owned merchant ships be consulted to allow for special preferential reduced-fare transportation of exhibition goods, and to reduce boat and train fares, in order to reduce the burden and facilitate the promotion of national products, which is in the public interest. Respectfully submitted to the Ministry of Communications (the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Railways are similar)."

Yangzhou National Exhibition Closing: The association's participation in the Jiangdu County National Products Exhibition, with a duration of three weeks, has reached its expiration date and is scheduled to close today. Liu Zhongying, a standing committee member of the association, took an early train to the province yesterday morning to host the closing ceremony of the National Products Exhibition. According to Chen Binghui, a standing committee member of the association, the Yangzhou National Exhibition was not as prosperous as the Zhenjiang exhibition due to the continuous autumn rain after the opening. According to statistics, the total business volume in three weeks was more than 134,200 yuan, and the total number of visitors was more than 118,100. Yesterday, the association requested the Shanghai North Station and Zhenjiang Station to allocate hanging cars to transport the remaining goods and items from the Yangzhou exhibition, and was deeply grateful. Now, the Jiangdu County National Products Exhibition, which was continued by this association from Zhenjiang to Yangzhou, has reached its expiration date and is scheduled to close on the 25th of this month. There are about 200 participating manufacturers who plan to return to Shanghai by train from Zhenjiang Station on the 27th of this month. Because there are still many remaining goods and items, we request your office to allocate two hanging cars to drive to Zhenjiang for loading. The time will be determined by your office, and the ticket prices will also be discounted as usual. A corresponding letter is hereby sent, hoping that you will investigate and reply accordingly.

Zhenjiang Exhibition Income and Expenditure Accounts: The Zhenjiang National Exhibition previously held by the association closed on the 26th of last month. All income and expenditure accounts of the National Exhibition handled by the association have been settled. Yesterday, the association specially submitted a report to the Jiangsu Provincial Party Department, the Provincial Government, the Shanghai Municipal Party Department, and the Municipal Social Bureau for record. The original submission stated: "Submitting a report regarding the matter. This association led the Shanghai National Products Manufacturers Touring Group to participate in the Jiangsu Provincial Capital National Products Exhibition on August 1st, which closed on August 26th. All income and expenditure accounts have been settled. The total income was 5,156 yuan, 6 jiao, and 1 cent. The total expenditure was 5,539 yuan, 8 jiao, and 4 fen. The Sixth Round of British Boxer Indemnity Bond Fund Custody Committee Held Yesterday 137

Held on the Third Floor of the Central Bank

Agreed to Improve Various Lottery Methods

According to the Shen Shi News Agency, the Sixth Round of British Boxer Indemnity Bond Fund Custody Committee has held two regular meetings on July 12th and August 27th. The committee held its third regular meeting yesterday on the third floor of the Central Bank, decided on the lottery date and location, and improved the lottery method. The details are as follows:

Attendees: The Sixth Round of British Boxer Indemnity Custody Committee held its third regular meeting yesterday at 2:00 a.m. The attendees included Xu Kan and Jiang Lufu, representatives of the Ministry of Finance; Zhang Jingli and Chen Yaozu, representatives of the Ministry of Railways; Ren Yingzhong, representative of the Auditing Department; Zeng Rongpu and Xia Pingfang (substituting for) Maxwell, representatives of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee; Jin Guoshi, representative of the Ministry of Communications; Xia Pingfang, representative of the Bank of China; Chen Duan, representative of the Central Bank; and Gatsby, representative of HSBC. The meeting was chaired by Xu Kan and adjourned at around 5:00 p.m.

Key Resolutions: At the beginning of the meeting, the chairman reported on the committee's affairs, and then the discussion began. The key resolutions were: (1) The date for the first round of principal repayment lottery was decided to be held at 10:00 a.m. on the 15th of next month; (2) The lottery location was set on the third floor of the Central Bank; (3) The lottery method was decided to be divided into groups to give everyone hope of winning; (4) Regarding the lottery date, it was decided to publish it in various newspapers today to make it known to the public.

Lottery Method: After the meeting, Chen Duan, the representative of the Central Bank, said that the total amount of the bond was 1.3 million yuan, with face values of 50 pounds, 100 pounds, and 1,000 pounds, with 2,000 bonds of 50 pounds, 4,000 bonds of 100 pounds, and 1,000 bonds of 1,000 pounds, totaling 7,000 bonds. In order to give everyone a chance to win, the lottery will be divided into seven groups, allocated according to the number of each type of bond, with two groups drawn from the 2,000 bonds, four groups from the 4,000 bonds, and one group from the 1,000 bonds. Every 1,000 numbers of each type will have a chance to win, so that the chance of winning can be equalized.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Re-Wires the Executive Yuan and Ministry to Recover the Pilotage Management Right 138

Appealing to Comply with Public Sentiment

And Not to Repeat Past Malpractices

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce has repeatedly telegraphed the government to strive to recover the pilotage management right. Yesterday, it wired the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and other agencies, stating: "To the esteemed Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing. On the 22nd of this month, we received a letter from the Preparatory Committee of the Chinese Pilots Association stating that the Interim Regulations on Pilotage Management, which were formulated by the government in September of last year, were soon opposed by customs advisors who advocated revision and sought the opinions of various countries on whether they agreed to determine the course of action. The authorities, adhering to their instructions, distorted and changed the pilotage regulations again and again. The important points of the original regulations were almost entirely altered, such as allowing them to maintain the existing positions of foreign pilots and stipulating that new foreign pilots could still be employed when necessary. The management right and the examination right must be subject to others. The right does not belong to us, and we are also willing to tie our own hands diplomatically, creating a coordinated situation. The so-called recovery of pilotage is a line of hope that has been cut off from this point. Our association, having received reliable information from the foreign side, has repeatedly reported the situation in telegrams to the Executive Yuan and the Executive Yuan, requesting that the revised regulations be submitted to relevant groups for joint study before they are approved and promulgated. However, our voices were hoarse, and our appeals were ignored until we were ignored. The current situation is such that the result is foreseeable. It is now heard that the revised new regulations will be implemented on the 1st of next month. If they are allowed to be promulgated, a big mistake will be made. With the strength of the Chinese people, there is no way to save it. Therefore, we specially prepare a letter to present the situation and request your association to vehemently state the advantages and disadvantages and strive again. If it is not adopted, please announce the entire process of recovering the pilotage to the people of the country to see that your association's participation by representatives is based on protecting the country as a prerequisite and does not go along with those who eat meat, so as not to take the blame for others and to avoid being a scapegoat. In terms of merit and crime, there will be public opinion for thousands of years. We dare to base our advice on the wise and speak frankly, and we hope that you will investigate and reply, which is truly desirable. The pilotage profession is related to maritime rights and military opportunities, no less than the lifeblood of a country. Sovereignty cannot be borrowed for a long time. If the right of management and examination is in the hands of foreigners, and new pilots can still be employed as usual, then the so-called recovery of the water management right is tantamount to buying a casket and returning the pearl. The government has repeatedly shown the people of the country that it will revise unequal treaties. If the General Regulations on Pilotage in various ports, which have no treaty basis, are subject to foreign interference and cannot be thoroughly revised, then the so-called revision of treaties is no different from a mirage and is even more distant. How can we comfort the aspirations of hundreds of millions of people? Therefore, we do not avoid bothering you and make our final appeal to urge the Executive Yuan and the Ministry to weigh the advantages and disadvantages and comply with public sentiment, and not to let the malpractices of the General Regulations on Pilotage of 1907 be seen again today and become an indelible scar in diplomatic history. This is our most sincere prayer. Respectfully, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

Chamber of Commerce Re-Wires the Ministry of Finance to Oppose the Scrapping of Old Stamp Tax Tickets 139

Merchants' Pre-Paid Tax Payments Should Not Be Confiscated

Please Allow Exchange for New Stamps to Alleviate Merchants' Difficulties

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce re-wired the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating: "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance in Nanjing. In accordance with the Ministry's announcement that new stamp tax tickets will be issued starting from November 1st of this year, and the old stamp tax tickets will be abolished, our association previously received letters and telegrams from the Jinhua County Chamber of Commerce and the Jiaxing County Chamber of Commerce in Zhejiang Province, requesting that we forward them to withdraw the order. We wired the Ministry on the 12th of this month. Recently, we received a telegram from the Zhenhai County Chamber of Commerce in Zhejiang Province on the 21st of this month, stating that our members in the money industry, pawn industry, sauce garden, etc., have successively sent letters stating that they were shocked to read the Ministry of Finance's announcement that new stamp tax tickets with pagoda patterns will be issued starting from November 1st, and at the same time, all old stamps will be abolished and cannot be used again, and those who violate this will be punished. Since many years ago, merchants have been forced to purchase stamps by the collection agencies, resulting in a large number of accumulated stamps. Although they reluctantly purchased them at that time, they were originally intended for daily use. Even if there are accumulated stamps, they can still be temporarily used as assets. Once they are abolished, the loss will be unbearable. Our association members vow not to recognize this and request your association to argue for it according to reason, etc., arriving at the association. Based on this, the association convened an emergency executive committee meeting to discuss it. It was unanimously agreed that stamp tax tickets are issued by the government. If old tickets can be abolished due to the issuance of new tickets, then all valuable securities and bank notes can be issued and abolished at will. The government can obtain a huge amount of illegal income, but the people cannot bear the illegal marrow extraction. Is this tolerable? What is not tolerable? The case concerns the merchants' pain and suffering. Therefore, we are calling on your help. It was resolved that in addition to wiring the Ministry of Finance to amend the order and allow the continued use of accumulated stamps or allow the exchange of new stamps, we specially wire your association to take effective action immediately until the goal is achieved, etc. On the same day, we also received telegrams from the Chaichiao Township Chamber of Commerce in Zhenhai County on the 21st of this month, stating the same reasons, etc. We have approved these. It is found that the stamp tax is a national tax, and merchants have purchased and accumulated a large number of stamps as a pre-payment of taxes, which is a virtue of being brave in paying taxes and should be commended. Now, their pre-paid tax payments are confiscated and invalidated, and they are required to pay again. There is nothing more unfair than this. Moreover, the stamp tax tickets should be deemed to have completed the tax payment at the time of use and cancellation. If new tickets are issued and old tickets are prohibited, it is not the government's intention to show compassion for merchants and encourage tax payment. Therefore, we re-wire the Ministry for review and humbly request that the order be withdrawn and that the old tickets continue to be valid, or that the old tickets be allowed to be exchanged for new tickets to alleviate the merchants' difficulties. Respectfully, Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China."

The United Shipping Vessel Sold, and the Placement of Workers Resolved 142

Thirty-Five People Hired

The Rest are Dismissed with Compensation

The sale of the United Shipping Vessel by Jardine Matheson & Co. to the Sanbei Company has not been resolved due to the company's failure to arrange for the placement of workers in the middle cabin, stevedoring, stoker, and steward departments in advance. Yesterday, Sun Lvpian, a committee member of the Seafarers' Association, together with Zhao Banfu, secretary of the General Association, Yu Qiaqing of the Sanbei General Manager's Office, and Ban Daote of Jardine Matheson & Co., negotiated a resolution. The remaining employees in various departments will be given compensation and dismissed, and all workers will be ordered to leave the ship. Sanbei will also inspect and accept it according to the procedures. The dispute has been resolved.

Qian Peigao's Revenge Case Confirmed by An'nan County 143

The Lawyers' Association Has Submitted a Petition for Amnesty

In October of last year, student Qian Peigao, in order to avenge his father, stabbed He Zunfu, the former magistrate of An'nan County, Guizhou Province, at the Golden Grand Theater on Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession. The court sentenced Qian to seven years in prison. Qian's defense lawyer, Qian Shusheng, checked the files and Qian's confession and suggested that Qian's conduct was commendable and requested the Shanghai Lawyers' Association to forward it to the Executive Yuan of the National Government for the issuance of an amnesty. This has been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that Qian Peigao's assassination of He Zunfu was indeed to avenge his father, as confirmed by the current magistrate of An'nan County, Yan Shibin, in his reply to the court's inquiry. The original letter is extracted below. The Second Special District Court sent a letter to An'nan County investigating several points: (1) Summon Chen Guangjiong, Ma Shenxiang, Guo Yiguang, Chou Zhushi, Jiang Nanhai, etc., to the county to inquire about why Qian Bing (i.e., Qian Bin) was shot by Zhou Haitao of the An'nan County garrison or framed by Magistrate He Zunfu. (2) Inquire whether the above persons are gentry in An'nan County. (3) Summon Qian Bing's wife, Dai, to the case to inquire about the reason for her husband's murder and who killed him. (4) Whether Qian Bing served as the Director of the Finance Bureau when He Zunfu was the magistrate of An'nan County, and whether he borrowed 1,000 yuan and 400 taels of opium from him, etc. We have checked and found that Chen Guangjie, Shu Zhushi, etc., are indeed local gentry in An'nan County. At that time, the gentry and Xian Bing's wife and merchant Liu Ziyuan and others were summoned for inquiry, and the statements were recorded separately. However, after investigation, former Magistrate He Zunfu colluded with garrison commander Zhou Haitao to secretly shoot the Director of the Finance Bureau Qian Bing without specifying what crime Qian Bing had committed and reported it to the senior government for verification of the case. There was no case to be found. This case was actually caused by the failure of former Magistrate He's request and the hatred of his brother He Yingxian, which led to bribing the garrison to assassinate Qian Bing. At that time, our county magistrate was the battalion commander of the Third Battalion of the Fifth Regiment of the Second Division of the National Revolutionary Army. After the incident, he was ordered to station in An'nan County, so he knew the inside story. However, for the sake of caution, he specially reported it to Liu Mingxiang, the senior officer of the An'nan garrison at the time, to make it clear. We have received a reply from Brigade Commander Liu stating that He's case was handled entirely by He alone, and the military had nothing to do with it. When Qian Bing was executed, he also asked Zhou Haitao, who was stationed in the county, to supervise the execution. Now that the Shanghai court has inquired, your brother can tell the truth. It has nothing to do with the military. We believe that there are regulations for homicide, but Qian Bing's son killed He Zunfu because of his father's irreconcilable hatred, and his filial piety is commendable. Your Honor advocates justice and preserves Qian Peigao's filial piety, which is truly a public service. The Shanghai Lawyers' Association also believes that Qian's filial piety is commendable and has submitted a document to the Executive Yuan requesting the issuance of an amnesty and has submitted the entire case file to the Executive Yuan for verification.

Yixing County People Beg Various Sectors for Relief 146

Yixing County's terrain is backed by mountains and faces lakes, and most of the fields are high-lying. This year, it has suffered a severe drought, and the disaster has been particularly severe. It is learned that the local gentry in the county have organized the Yixing County Drought Relief Association and issued a tearful appeal on behalf of the hundreds of thousands of starving people in the county, stating: "To charity groups and philanthropists across the country, Yixing is located between the three major river basins of Taihu Lake, Tao Lake, and Ge Lake, and has always been known as a water town. In previous years, floods have been a disaster, and we have only known how to prevent water disasters. But this year is very different. From spring to summer to autumn, except for two rains of an inch or so during Arbor Day and World Labor Day, it has been sunny and rainless. During the Dragon Boat Festival and the summer solstice, which is the busiest time, the weather was abnormal, and it was suddenly extremely hot, fanned by strong winds and exposed to the scorching sun, causing the planting season to be delayed, the unmown wheat fields to crack, and the sown rice to wither. The local gentry raised a large sum of money to purchase motor boats, and they were also blessed by the authorities, who allocated more boats to rescue them with all their might. Eventually, the rivers and canals became land, and all previous efforts were abandoned. It is even more lamentable that tens of thousands of acres of fertile land have turned into stone, and thousands of miles of red land have turned into barren land. It is truly a strange event in the past for a water town to suffer such a severe drought. It is difficult to obtain drinking water, let alone irrigation. It has become a major problem related to human life. Now it is the autumnal equinox, which is usually the time for harvesting. Only then did we get thunderstorms, but they were less than a foot deep. The withered rice in the fields, although revived, is not fruitful. The replanted by-products, although sown, do not sprout. Looking around the county, hundreds of thousands of starving refugees, sleeping in the open and eating in the wind, are wandering aimlessly. Groups are forming and venturing into danger. Among them, nine out of ten houses are empty, and there are those who have no money to lend. There are those who are in imminent danger. Some have not eaten for several days and have starved to death. Some are reluctantly begging for food, and some have developed a pessimistic attitude and have even committed suicide with their families. What crime have the people of Yixing committed to suffer such suffering? It is cruel and tragic. If water demons are at work, there is still an autumn harvest to rely on. If the drought demon is prevalent, there is complete despair, and it is difficult to survive. From 1907 to 1932, we have suffered from floods, typhoons, insect plagues, and the disasters of war in the year of the Jiazi. The warehouses in the entire area have long been depleted, and all public funds have been exhausted. The vitality has not been restored, but Heaven has not helped us. We are now facing the greatest and most unprecedented drought in the history of Yixing. A great catastrophe has come, and grief is everywhere. Without seeking help, how can we be renewed? We are exhausted and have launched a fundraising campaign and made a drought disaster film. In addition to recommending representatives to present to the authorities to beg for help, we hope that the people of the Party and the country, as well as various charitable organizations, institutions, and great philanthropists, will not tire of doing good, embrace each other, and see the prevalence of benevolence and the widespread praise. We also ask you to generously donate to help the remnants. The merits are immeasurable. We respectfully bow our heads and appeal to you from the bottom of our hearts. The entire staff of the Yixing Drought Relief Committee."

Western Shanghai Residents Oppose the French Municipal Council Building a Sewer in Xujiahui 147

The Puzhao River is one of the largest currents in this port, with the Zhaojiabang to the east and the Puhuitang to the west. Due to the proliferation of factories on the west bank of the Zhaojiabang, wastewater accumulated. Two years ago, Ma Xiangbo and others suggested that the Tianyao Bridge dam be changed into a channel, exiting southward through the Caohejing Port from the small gate. Since its dredging, the source has been clean, and the people have benefited. Unexpectedly, the French Municipal Council, for some unknown reason, is building a very large sewer in the west of Xujiahui, intending to discharge all the wastewater of the entire concession through it. What was once clean will soon become polluted again. Therefore, the people suddenly became alarmed. Yesterday, the Puhuitang Promotion Committee held a meeting at Gu's residence in Chengjiaqiao. More than 60 people attended, including Gu Rungui, Yang Fuyuan, Pan Boxian, Tang Puzhuang (from Shanghai), Shen Caigeng, Li Wenlai, Li Qixian, Gu Junjie (from Songjiang), Yang Xueqiao, Wang Jingsheng, Wang Daoxing, and Jin Qiancheng (from Qingpu). Gu Rungui was elected as chairman, and Tang Puzhuang as the recorder. The chairman first announced the purpose of the meeting. For a time, the crowd was filled with anger. As a result, it was resolved that Ma Xiangbo would take the lead in submitting a petition to the municipal government and sending a letter to the Chinese directors of the French Municipal Council, explaining the advantages and disadvantages, in the hope that the sewer outlet would be moved and the sewage would flow eastward, not into the inland. Otherwise, they would build a dam foundation in Tushanwan to prevent the sewage from flowing westward as a last resort.

Western Dye Merchants Contract to Sell Japanese Indigo Coming to Shanghai 151

Wu Xingzai and Others of the Chengzhi Store Organize the Far East Trading Company

Someone Sent a Bomb and a Warning Letter the Day Before Yesterday

Last month, the Shanghai Western Dye Industry Association suddenly received a confidential letter signed by the National Youth Corps and another anonymous letter accusing businesses such as Chengzhi Wu Xingzai, Ruitai Li Shuyan, Ruihe Wu Renbao, Yukang Wang Pengcheng, Dehe Gongji Qiu Hongsheng, and Gonghe Lai Shenqinshun of contracting with Japanese merchants to sell 3 million taels of indigo under the name of the Far East Trading Company, attempting to monopolize the market. The industry association, not wanting to ignore this, convened a meeting to discuss how to deal with the situation, as reported in the previous newspaper. However, no progress has been seen so far. The following is a description of the investigation. People who care about society will certainly not take it lightly.

Organizing a New Company It is reported that the aforementioned businesses organized the Far East Trading Company specifically to contract the sale of Japanese indigo. To avoid contract disputes with De Fu Yanghang, Nanxing Yanghang, and Ciba Dye Factory, it was decided that the Far East Trading Company would come forward to contract the sale from Japan, while they secretly manipulated it. The total amount was indeed 3 million taels, which was divided and stockpiled by the businesses, with the intention of speculating in case of emergency.

Goods to Be Shipped According to reliable information received yesterday, the original price of the Japanese indigo was 50 taels per barrel, meaning that 3 million taels would amount to a huge 60,000 barrels. The goods were originally scheduled to be delivered in early this month. However, after being discovered by others and the German merchant De Fu Yanghang raised serious questions to the contracting businesses, fearing complications, the matter was temporarily shelved invisibly. However, it is still being pursued vigorously in secret, and it is possible that it will arrive in Shanghai in the near future.

Seizing the Opportunity to Manipulate It is said that the businesses' intention to contract Japanese indigo was due to the instability of the situation in the Far East. They predicted that once the situation in the Far East broke out, the source of German indigo would be difficult to obtain. At that time, they could hoard the rare goods and make ten times the original purchase price. At the same time, with the needs of the market, they could seize the opportunity to manipulate it for a while.

A Bomb After this incident, although the businesses once published a notice in the newspaper to deny it, because there was no thorough investigation and no results were announced, they were still not understood by some people. As a result, a bomb was suddenly sent to Chengzhi Dye Store the day before yesterday, along with a warning letter. Although the contents of the letter have not been seen, it is speculated that it is nothing more than patriotic action.

Setting Up a Tide Gauge Outside Wusong Estuary 152

Located at Tongsha Sandbar

Under Construction

Tidal rise and fall is most closely related to merchant ships. The rise and fall of sea tides outside the Wusong Estuary is essential knowledge for coastal ships. However, until now, there has been no tide gauge installed, which is a major shortcoming. In view of this, the Hydrographic Office of the Navy Department is building a tide gauge base on the sandbar of Tongsha in the sea outside Wusong. A tide gauge with a displacement of 100 tons made of cement is being sunk on the Tongsha sandbar. At the lowest tide, it can be seen 8 feet above the water, and at high tide, it is level with the sea surface. The position of the tide gauge is 88.5 degrees due north of the Nanhui surveying marker, at 122 degrees 6 minutes east longitude and 31 degrees 5 minutes north latitude. A unmanned light has now been installed on the base. Once the weather is calm, workers and technicians will be sent to the base to install a marker post and install a sea tide gauge to telegraph the daily tide rise and fall to various sea vessels at any time, in order to reduce the risk of merchant ships grounding. The location of the tide gauge base is outside the hydrographic route and has nothing to do with ships traveling to and from Shanghai and other routes. The installation of this project is truly good news for the shipping industry in this port.

Chen Jiying Discusses Huang Huancheng's Disappearance 154

Full Text of the Ten Articles of His Handwritten Voluntary Letter

Details Huang's Relationship with Women

Since the disappearance of lawyer Huang Huancheng, this newspaper has disclosed it, and various newspapers have also published it in succession. However, according to a report in a certain newspaper the day before yesterday, Huang himself is now in Zhenjiang and has sent a letter to his colleague lawyer Zhang Shiying, who explained the reasons for Huang's sudden abandonment of his family and solo escape. In order to carefully investigate the matter, this reporter specially visited the main character in this case, Ms. Chen Jiying from Yixing, and Mr. Zhou, the main introducer of Huang and Chen's marriage at the time, and obtained a lot of materials. The details are recorded below.

Ms. Chen's Words Yesterday afternoon, the reporter visited Ms. Chen Jiying and obtained the following conversation (the following are all Ms. Chen's words): I met Huang last winter through the introduction of Mr. Zhou Jingming and Mr. Zheng Shengguang. At that time, Huang was very flattering and vowed to marry me as his wife. Because Huang was of high birth and had a good practice, I agreed to his request. Huang also claimed that it was his first marriage and that he was only 27 years old. However, for the sake of prudence, when we got married this spring, in addition to the two introducers, Zhou and Zheng, I specially asked for proof from many people to be cautious.

Huang Huancheng, Chen Jiying, Li Huifang

Voluntary Letter Chen said that she immediately took out a handwritten voluntary letter from Huang and showed it to me. It is transcribed as follows: I, Huang Huancheng, am 27 years old, born on the 19th day of the tenth month at Chen time, Chen Jiying, 22 years old, born on the 13th day of the eighth month at You time, because both parties are in love and voluntarily grow old together, and the conditions are listed on the right: (1) After signing this voluntary letter, the woman is a member of the man's family, and the man shall bear the woman's lifelong living expenses, etc. (2) Both parties voluntarily grow old together for life, and neither party may repent halfway unless one party violates this agreement. (3) The woman must continue her studies, and all expenses shall be provided by the man. (4) The man shall be responsible for supporting the woman's mother, and shall not be responsible for supporting anyone other than the woman's mother. (5) This matter is not a sale or abduction, and the parties may not sue, and outsiders may not use this to blackmail. (6) Children born after the signing of this voluntary letter shall be regarded as legitimate children. (7) The woman shall follow the man into the countryside, but the man shall not leave the woman alone in a foreign country without reason. (8) After signing this agreement, both parties shall not engage in any improper or immoral behavior, and each may supervise and advise each other. (9) The man shall give the woman a gift of 300 yuan. (10) This agreement is made in duplicate, and each party shall hold one as proof. February 10, 23rd year of the Republic of China, Huang Huancheng (signed), Chen Jiying (signed), Witness for the man: Ling Wenjie (inserted), Witness for the woman: Chen Chu (ten), Introducer: Wang Chunyang (correct), Lü Haiqing (ten), Wang Qingshan (ten), Tang Hongjun (ten), Zhou Jingming (signed), Zheng Shengguang (inserted).

The Cui and Zhang Families Chen continued, "Since my marriage to Huang, I gradually saw a big change in Huang's attitude, and Huang was very secretive about letters from his family. I became suspicious and paid attention to everything. Once, Huang's relatives came to Shanghai from Taizhou, and I took the opportunity to inquire about his family affairs. I learned that Huang was indeed married in his hometown, and his wife, Ms. Cui, had already given birth to a son and a daughter. In the 18th year of the Republic of China, when Huang came to Shanghai and worked as a professor at Yalu Middle School, he seduced a woman surnamed Zhang from a good family outside the North Gate of Taizhou and brought her to Shanghai, sending Zhang to the Kunfan Girls' School on Mei Bai Ke Road. At that time, Huang also vowed to marry Zhang, but Huang abandoned her after the event. Later, the woman surnamed Zhang returned to her hometown in frustration and has now become mentally ill due to anger."

Another Marriage Contract She took out a photo and a marriage invitation card and showed them to me. On the photo, the words "Brother Huancheng, Sister Li Huifang" were written in pen. The invitation card reads "Huancheng and Huifang, introduced by Mr. Chen Maoyun and Mr. Peng Tiehu, with the consent of both parties and the permission of the parents, will be engaged on December 14, 19th year of the Republic of China. We hereby inform you, Huang Huancheng and Li Huifang." According to Chen, Huang was also engaged to this Ms. Li, but was later abandoned by Huang. Therefore, when Huang practiced law in Shanghai, whenever a client asked him to publish a notice in the newspaper, Huang always used the three words "Lawyer Huang" and did not dare to use the two words "Huancheng" at first, fearing that Ms. Li would come to ask questions.

Two Points of Explanation Chen finally stated that Huang's intention to abandon me this time has become an undeniable fact. As for someone saying that I have bad habits, or that I am a concubine discarded by an official, and that these were the reasons for Huang's departure, it is not worth the laughter of connoisseurs. Regarding the first point, I have given up smoking cigarettes in recent months, let alone other things. As for the second point, it is even more nonsense. Even if I had both, I might as well formally divorce, so why run away quietly, like an escape? This is something that even a fool would not do, let alone Huang, who is a lawyer? Now I have decided to argue, on the one hand, to seek legal solutions, and on the other hand, to ask for social assistance. I will not give up until I achieve my goal.

The Words of the Introducer At this point, the reporter excused himself and went to visit the introducer, Mr. Zhou Jingming. According to him, I (Zhou Jun refers to himself) am a cousin of Huang, but we have been apart for a long time and do not know much about Huang's family affairs. If I had known that Huang had a wife at that time, I would never have been willing to be a puppet. In short, Huang's departure without saying goodbye and abandoning Ms. Chen is inconsistent with morality and human relations. However, for the sake of protecting Huang, I deeply hope that he can repent as soon as possible, return to Shanghai immediately, and negotiate formally, so as to avoid the expansion of the situation and cause grief.

The number of plague-infected pigs that died of illness reached as many as 70 to 80. From July, August, and September, there were more than 4,000 in total. Therefore, the dead pig oil refining factory could not cook and refine them in time, and the rotten dead pigs were buried on the spot, causing a foul odor to spread, which was unbearable to smell and made people feel like vomiting for three months. All Chinese and Western people who come to Song to visit the seaside cover their noses and pass by. Tang Chengzong, the Wusong Municipal Committee member, has reported to the municipal government for the sake of public health, requesting the relocation of the oil refining factory and other details, which has been reported by this newspaper. Since mid-September, the weather has turned cold and the number of plague-infected pigs has decreased greatly, but there are still more than ten a day. However, the daily accumulation of dead pigs, internal organs, and other rotten and smelly things is not a small number. The Health Bureau Inspection Office has great difficulties in dealing with the problem of disposing of these filthy objects. It is said that the plan proposed in the absence of a solution is to build a huge concrete pond near the oil refining factory to store dead pigs' internal organs and other things to prevent the odor from overflowing, and then find a way to transport them to a distant place for burial. A special report has been submitted to the municipal government for approval. It is heard that the municipal government has ordered the Public Works Bureau to send personnel to Song to assess the situation the day before yesterday. However, the cost of building the pond is about 1,000 yuan. At present, the Health Bureau is unable to raise such a large sum of money in a short period of time and is currently deliberating.

Kidnapped by Bandits Three and a Half Years Ago and Killed for Ransom

Received a Telegram from Tianjin the Day Before Yesterday Asking His Wife to Go and Identify the Body

The Yisheng Wheel, a regular passenger ship of the British-owned Jardine Matheson, which runs between Shanghai and Tianjin, and the comprador of the ship, Li Shanting, and Chen Zhuting, the Tianjin dock manager of Jardine, were kidnapped by bandits three years ago and extorted for a large sum of money. Chen Zhuting paid a ransom of 50,000 yuan, but was still killed for ransom. The body was only found after two years. At that time, Chen Zhuting's family found two locker keys in the deceased's belongings, which proved that it was indeed Chen's body. However, Li Shanting's body has been obtained by the bandits, but his remains are still missing. Li's family used an empty coffin to replace Li's clothes and hats for burial, and tried to find them. It has been three and a half years since the incident. Unexpectedly, a telegram suddenly arrived in Shanghai from Tianjin, saying that Li Shanting's body had been found and asking Li's wife to go to Tianjin to identify it in person as soon as possible. The method of identification will also be based on the belongings he left behind. After Li's wife received the report, she took a boat to Tianjin yesterday to identify the body, and then handed it over to the Dingsheng Wheel to be transported to Shanghai for burial. It is also learned that the passengers on the Yisheng Wheel who were kidnapped are now in negotiations with the bandits to redeem their tickets. It is heard that the place of negotiation is still a certain seaport in Hainan.

The Procedures for Reporting Marriages, Births, Deaths, etc. of Employees and Residents Within the Railway Boundary 159

The Model Form is Established by the Jingcha (Railway Police) Department

And Submitted to the Railway Bureau for Approval and Implementation

Xin She reported that the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Interior Affairs believe that the functions and responsibilities of local police and railway police are different, and that their powers and responsibilities are different. In order to ensure that both parties perform their duties and abide by their boundaries, they will count the regulations for local police and railway police service and compliance. The Railway Police Department stated that with regard to the application and reporting of marriage, birth, death, migration, construction, and other matters of employees and residents living within the railway boundary as stipulated in Articles 4 and 5 of the regulations, there are no prescribed procedures. It is specially proposed to establish the following formats: (1) Railway Boundary Resident Birth Report Form, (2) Railway Boundary Resident Death Diagnosis Certificate, (3) Railway Boundary Resident Marriage Report Form, (4) Railway Boundary Resident Household Migration Report Form, (5) Railway Boundary Resident Building Application Form, and submit them to the Railway Bureau for approval and implementation.
